MEE6: Prefix: !
!servers - Gets a list of all available private servers. You must be ranked to use this command.
!expertservers - Gets a list of private servers available to those with an expert rank.
!testserver - A link to the test server.

DYNO: Prefix: ?
?suggestionhelp - How do I make a suggestion?  Aliases: ?shelp, ?suggesthelp 
?rankhelp - How do I get a rank?  Aliases: ?rhelp 
?ranks - Gets a list of all available colour ranks to join. This command can only be run in the <#519624169730605086> channel.
?rank [colour] - Join a colour rank. This command can only be run in the <#519624169730605086> channel.

CARL-BOT: Prefix: &
&suggest [suggestion] - Submits a suggestion to <#507673335816126509>. You must have the ranked role in order to use this command. (?shelp)

RYTHM Prefix: =
=p [name/url] - Adds a song to the play queue.  Aliases: =play 
=q [page num] - Get the current play queue.  Aliases: =queue 
=s - Vote to skip the current song.  Aliases: =skip 
=np - Gets the current song that's playing.  Aliases: =nowplaying

Both bomb types release large quantities of energy from relatively small amounts of matter.
The¬†first test¬†of a fission ("atomic") bomb released an amount of energy approximately equal to 20,000¬†tons of TNT¬†(84¬†TJ).[1]¬†The first thermonuclear ("hydrogen") bomb¬†test¬†released energy approximately equal to 10¬†million tons of TNT (42¬†PJ). Nuclear bombs have had¬†yields¬†between 10 tons TNT (the¬†W54) and 50 megatons for the¬†Tsar Bomba¬†(see¬†TNT equivalent). A thermonuclear weapon weighing little more than 2,400 pounds (1,100¬†kg) can release energy equal to more than 1.2¬†million tons of TNT (5.0¬†PJ).[2]
A nuclear device no larger than a conventional bomb can devastate an entire city by blast, fire, and¬†radiation. Since they are¬†weapons of mass destruction, the¬†proliferation of nuclear weapons¬†is a focus of¬†international relations¬†policy. Nuclear weapons have been deployed twice in war, by the United States¬†against the Japanese cities of Hiroshima and Nagasaki¬†in 1945 during¬†World War II.
